IN A RECENT SURVEY ADMINISTERED BY THE UNIVERSITY OF CALIFORNIA 29% OF STUDENTS REPORTED SUICIDAL BEHAVIOR. 21% OF STUDENTS REPORTED DEPRESSION. 24% OF STUDENTS REPORTED ANXIETY AND 2% OF OUR STUDENTS REPORT BEING IN RECOVERY FROM ALCOHOL AND OTHER DRUG USE.
